<h1 class="firstHeading mw-first-heading" id="firstHeading"><span class="mw-page-title-main">面积</span></h1>
<div class="vector-body" id="bodyContent">
<div class="noprint" id="siteSub">维基百科，自由的百科全书</div>
<div id="contentSub"></div>
<div id="contentSub2"></div>
<div id="jump-to-nav"></div>
<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">跳到导航</a>
<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#searchInput">跳到搜索</a>
<div class="mw-body-content mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="zh"><div class="mw-parser-output"><p><b>面积</b>（英语：<span lang="en">Area</span>）是用作表示一个<a href="/wiki/%E6%9B%B2%E9%9D%A2" title="曲面">曲面</a>或<a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E9%9D%A2_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="平面 (数学)">平面</a><a href="/wiki/%E5%9B%BE%E5%BD%A2" title="图形">图形</a>所占范围的<a href="/wiki/%E9%87%8F_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="量 (数学)">量</a>，可看成是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%95%B7%E5%BA%A6" title="长度">长度</a>（一维度量）及<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%AB%94%E7%A9%8D" title="体积">体积</a>（三维度量）的二维类比。对三维立体图形而言，图形的边界的面积称为<a href="/wiki/%E8%A1%A8%E9%9D%A2%E7%A9%8D" title="表面积">表面积</a>。
</p><p><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E8%A8%88%E7%AE%97" title="计算">计算</a>各基本平面图形面积及基本立体图形的表面积公式早已为<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8F%A4%E5%B8%8C%E8%87%98" title="古希腊">古希腊</a>及古<a href="/wiki/%E4%B8%AD%E5%9C%8B" title="中国">中国</a><a href="/wiki/%E4%BA%BA" title="人">人</a>所熟知。
</p><p>面积在<a class="mw-disambig" href="/wiki/%E8%BF%91%E4%BB%A3" title="近代">近代</a><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E6%95%B8%E5%AD%B8" title="数学">数学</a>中占相当重要的角色。面积除与<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B9%BE%E4%BD%95%E5%AD%B8" title="几何学">几何学</a>及<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%BE%AE%E7%A9%8D%E5%88%86" title="微积分">微积分</a>有关外，亦与<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%B7%9A%E6%80%A7%E4%BB%A3%E6%95%B8" title="线性代数">线性代数</a>中的<a href="/wiki/%E8%A1%8C%E5%88%97%E5%BC%8F" title="行列式">行列式</a>有关。在<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%88%86%E6%9E%90%E5%AD%A6" title="分析学">分析学</a>中，平面的面积通常以<a href="/wiki/%E5%8B%92%E8%B4%9D%E6%A0%BC%E6%B5%8B%E5%BA%A6" title="勒贝格测度">勒贝格测度</a>（Lebesgue measure）<a href="/wiki/%E5%AE%9A%E4%B9%89" title="定义">定义</a>。
</p>
<div aria-labelledby="mw-toc-heading" class="toc" id="toc" role="navigation"><input class="toctogglecheckbox" id="toctogglecheckbox" role="button" style="display:none" type="checkbox"/><div class="toctitle" dir="ltr" lang="zh"><h2 id="mw-toc-heading">目录</h2><span class="toctogglespan"><label class="toctogglelabel" for="toctogglecheckbox"></label></span></div>

<h2><span id=".E9.95.B7.E6.96.B9.E5.BD.A2.E7.9A.84.E9.9D.A2.E7.A9.8D"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="长方形的面积">长方形的面积</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9D%A2%E7%A7%AF&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="编辑章节：长方形的面积">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:182px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:RectangleLengthWidth.svg"><img alt="A rectangle with length and width labelled" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="170" data-file-width="220" decoding="async" height="139" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/RectangleLengthWidth.svg/180px-RectangleLengthWidth.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/RectangleLengthWidth.svg/270px-RectangleLengthWidth.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8d/RectangleLengthWidth.svg/360px-RectangleLengthWidth.svg.png 2x" width="180"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:RectangleLengthWidth.svg" title="放大"></a></div>这个长方形的面积是 <style data-mw-deduplicate="TemplateStyles:r58896141">.mw-parser-output .serif{font-family:Times,serif}</style><span class="serif"><span class="texhtml mvar" style="font-style:italic;margin-left:2px;margin-right:2px;">lw</span></span>.</div></div></div>
<p>最基本的面积公式是<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E9%95%B7%E6%96%B9%E5%BD%A2" title="长方形">长方形</a>的公式。当<i>l</i>是长，<i>w</i>是宽时，其公式为：<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AF_2-4"><a href="#cite_note-AF-2">[2]</a></sup>
</p><p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A=lw}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>l</mi>
<mi>w</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A=lw}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A=lw" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a4e209a0c2b0858ba101c9784d91b17c82851998" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:7.199ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>
</p><p>当其图形是一个<a href="/wiki/%E6%AD%A3%E6%96%B9%E5%BD%A2" title="正方形">正方形</a>时，<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle l=w}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>l</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>w</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle l=w}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="l = w" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/da2945b65218017b2513ae50e8191416582d7478" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:5.456ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，因此正方形的公式为：<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AF_2-5"><a href="#cite_note-AF-2">[2]</a></sup>
</p><p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A=s^{2}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<msup>
<mi>s</mi>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mn>2</mn>
</mrow>
</msup>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A=s^{2}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A=s^2" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/1607109864e43a307cc541ff06b73a7bfe423500" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.986ex; height:2.676ex;"/></span>
</p><p>长方形的面积计算方法需要证明。
</p>
<h4><span id=".E8.AD.89.E6.98.8E.5B5.5D"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="证明[5]">证明<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5"><a href="#cite_note-5">[5]</a></sup></span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9D%A2%E7%A7%AF&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="编辑章节：证明[5]">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:352px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Area_formula_of_rectangle.png"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="505" data-file-width="656" decoding="async" height="269" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Area_formula_of_rectangle.png/350px-Area_formula_of_rectangle.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/b/b2/Area_formula_of_rectangle.png/525px-Area_formula_of_rectangle.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/b/b2/Area_formula_of_rectangle.png 2x" width="350"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Area_formula_of_rectangle.png" title="放大"></a></div>证明</div></div></div>
<p><a href="/wiki/%E5%BC%95%E7%90%86" title="引理">引理</a>：两个长方形面积之比等于其长宽之积之比
</p><p>如图，根据《<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B9%BE%E4%BD%95%E5%8E%9F%E6%9C%AC" title="几何原本">几何原本</a>》第六卷命题一 ——等高之平行四边形的面积比与其底之比等同<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6"><a href="#cite_note-6">[6]</a></sup>，我们得到
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\begin{aligned}B:Y&amp;=a:c\\&amp;=ad:cd{\text{（ 第 五 卷 命 题 十 五 ）}},\end{aligned}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle {\begin{aligned}B:Y&amp;=a:c\\&amp;=ad:cd{\text{（ 第 五 卷 命 题 十 五 ）}},\end{aligned}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/8de49bd18b83d09aaa4532af70025dceefd95693" style="vertical-align: -2.671ex; width:33.972ex; height:6.509ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>又
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle {\begin{aligned}Y:G&amp;=b:d\\&amp;=ab:ad{\text{（ 第 五 卷 命 题 十 五 ）}},\end{aligned}}}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle {\begin{aligned}Y:G&amp;=b:d\\&amp;=ab:ad{\text{（ 第 五 卷 命 题 十 五 ）}},\end{aligned}}}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle {\begin{aligned}Y:G&amp;=b:d\\&amp;=ab:ad{\text{（ 第 五 卷 命 题 十 五 ）}},\end{aligned}}}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/9d0b7c41999cffa80b1e3e33ce18f30d981f181a" style="vertical-align: -2.671ex; width:34.039ex; height:6.509ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>所以
</p>

<p>引理证毕。
</p><p>定理：长方形的面积等于其长宽之积
</p>
<dl><dd></dd></dl>
<p>根据引理，
A:R=lw:(1x1)
</p><p>定义<a href="/wiki/%E5%8D%95%E4%BD%8D%E6%AD%A3%E6%96%B9%E5%BD%A2" title="单位正方形">单位正方形</a>的面积为一平方单位。由于R是单位正方形，因此面积是一平方单位。将一平方单位代入R，得到：A:1=lw:1
</p>
<dl><dd><dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A=lw}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>l</mi>
<mi>w</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A=lw}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A=lw" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a4e209a0c2b0858ba101c9784d91b17c82851998" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:7.199ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span> （第五卷命题九）</dd></dl></dd></dl>
<p>（定理证毕）
</p>
<div class="thumb tleft"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:182px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:ParallelogramArea.svg"><img alt="A diagram showing how a parallelogram can be re-arranged into the shape of a rectangle" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="300" data-file-width="220" decoding="async" height="245" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/ParallelogramArea.svg/180px-ParallelogramArea.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/ParallelogramArea.svg/270px-ParallelogramArea.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/1/1c/ParallelogramArea.svg/360px-ParallelogramArea.svg.png 2x" width="180"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:ParallelogramArea.svg" title="放大"></a></div>面积相同</div></div></div>
<h4><span id=".E5.88.87.E5.89.B2.E5.9C.96.E5.BD.A2"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="切割图形">切割图形</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9D%A2%E7%A7%AF&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" title="编辑章节：切割图形">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<p>有些简单的公式可以切割的方式得出。
</p><p>例如平行四边形，可以切割成一个梯形和一个直角三角形，如同右图。如果三角形移到平行四边形的另一边，就可以变成一个长方形。因此，平行四边形的面积公式有点像长方形的：<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AF_2-6"><a href="#cite_note-AF-2">[2]</a></sup>
</p><p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A=bh}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>b</mi>
<mi>h</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A=bh}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A=bh" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/a18eb7585c8d8707e21afffb3b3a439ad7e7f83b" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:7.178ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>
</p>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:182px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:TriangleArea.svg"><img alt="A parallelogram split into two equal triangles" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="160" data-file-width="220" decoding="async" height="131" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/TriangleArea.svg/180px-TriangleArea.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/TriangleArea.svg/270px-TriangleArea.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/7/7c/TriangleArea.svg/360px-TriangleArea.svg.png 2x" width="180"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:TriangleArea.svg" title="放大"></a></div>两个全等三角形</div></div></div>
<p>至于同样的平行四边形可以分割为两个全等三角形。因此三角形的公式为：<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-AF_2-7"><a href="#cite_note-AF-2">[2]</a></sup>
</p><p><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A={\frac {1}{2}}bh}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>
<mo>=</mo>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mfrac>
<mn>1</mn>
<mn>2</mn>
</mfrac>
</mrow>
<mi>b</mi>
<mi>h</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A={\frac {1}{2}}bh}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="A = \frac{1}{2}bh" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/78bb1af1b9493a6b26955f711ae9b95a68f671be" style="vertical-align: -1.838ex; width:9.177ex; height:5.176ex;"/></span>
</p>
<h4><span id=".E5.9C.93.E5.BD.A2.E9.9D.A2.E7.A9.8D"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="圆形面积">圆形面积</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9D%A2%E7%A7%AF&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="编辑章节：圆形面积">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h4>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E5%9C%86%E7%9A%84%E9%9D%A2%E7%A7%AF" title="圆的面积">圆的面积</a></div>
<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:CircleArea.svg"><img alt="A circle divided into many sectors can be re-arranged roughly to form a parallelogram" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="260" data-file-width="240" decoding="async" height="238" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/CircleArea.svg/220px-CircleArea.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/CircleArea.svg/330px-CircleArea.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/f/fb/CircleArea.svg/440px-CircleArea.svg.png 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:CircleArea.svg" title="放大"></a></div>圆形可以分割为很多扇形</div></div></div>
<p>圆形面积公式是基于基本的面积公式，假设有一个半径为r的圆形，分成很多扇形，那一个扇形的面积就会很接近三角形，就像上图一样。如果分得够细小，就可以看到半径为r的圆形面积相等于一个高为r，底为πr的平行四边形。<sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Surveyor_7-0"><a href="#cite_note-Surveyor-7">[7]</a></sup>
</p><p>我们也可以用<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E7%A9%8D%E5%88%86" title="积分">积分</a>得到更肯定的答案。
</p>
<dl><dd><span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle A=2\int _{-r}^{r}{\sqrt {r^{2}-x^{2}}}\,dx=\pi r^{2}.}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>A</mi>

<mn>2</mn>
<msubsup>

<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle A=2\int _{-r}^{r}{\sqrt {r^{2}-x^{2}}}\,dx=\pi r^{2}.}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle A=2\int _{-r}^{r}{\sqrt {r^{2}-x^{2}}}\,dx=\pi r^{2}.}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/eec36ca9d982f6c005b888ef2830fe2b8312ce1e" style="vertical-align: -2.505ex; width:30.087ex; height:6.009ex;"/></span></dd></dl>
<p>计算不规则之图形面积，可用填补法或切割法来计算之。
</p>

<h2><span id=".E5.96.AE.E4.BD.8D.E5.88.97.E8.A1.A8"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="单位列表">单位列表</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9D%A2%E7%A7%AF&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="编辑章节：单位列表">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<h3><span id=".E4.B8.BB.E8.A6.81.E5.96.AE.E4.BD.8D"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="主要单位">主要单位</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9D%A2%E7%A7%AF&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="编辑章节：主要单位">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h3>
<p>面积的测量单位主要包括：
</p>
<ul><li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E6%96%B9%E5%85%AC%E9%87%8C" title="平方公里">平方公里</a>——1,000,000平方米</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%85%AC%E9%A0%83" title="公顷">平方公引</a>（ha）——10,000平方米</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E5%85%AC%E7%95%9D" title="公亩">平方公丈</a>（a）——100平方米</li>
<li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E6%96%B9%E5%85%AC%E5%B0%BA" title="平方公尺">平方公尺</a>——1平方米，<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%9C%8B%E9%9A%9B%E6%A8%99%E6%BA%96%E5%96%AE%E4%BD%8D" title="国际标准单位">国际标准单位</a></li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E6%96%B9%E5%88%86%E7%B1%B3" title="平方分米">平方公寸</a>——0.01平方米</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E6%96%B9%E5%8E%98%E7%B1%B3" title="平方厘米">平方公分</a>——0.0001平方分米</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E6%96%B9%E6%AF%AB%E7%B1%B3" title="平方毫米">平方公厘</a>——0.000001平方厘米</li></ul>
<p>市制：
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/%E7%95%9D" title="亩">亩</a>——10丈 × 6丈 ——33.33米 × 20米 ——666.67平方米</li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B9%B3%E6%96%B9%E5%B8%82%E9%87%8C&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="平方市里（页面不存在）">平方市里</a>——0.25平方公里</li>
<li><a class="new" href="/w/index.php?title=%E5%B9%B3%E6%96%B9%E5%B8%82%E5%B0%BA&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" title="平方市尺（页面不存在）">平方市尺</a>——1/9平方米</li></ul>
<p>台制：
</p>
<ul><li><a href="/wiki/%E7%94%B2_(%E5%96%AE%E4%BD%8D)" title="甲 (单位)">甲</a>——9,699.173平方公尺（平方米）</li>
<li><a href="/wiki/%E5%9D%AA" title="坪">坪</a>——3.3058平方公尺（平方米）</li></ul>
<p>香港：
</p>
<ul><li><a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%B9%B3%E6%96%B9%E5%91%8E" title="平方呎">平方呎</a>（平方英尺）——929平方厘米</li></ul>

<h2><span id=".E5.9A.B4.E6.A0.BC.E5.AE.9A.E7.BE.A9"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="严格定义">严格定义</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9D%A2%E7%A7%AF&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="编辑章节：严格定义">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
<div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">主条目：<a href="/wiki/%E8%8B%A5%E5%B0%94%E5%BD%93%E6%B5%8B%E5%BA%A6" title="若尔当测度">若尔当测度</a></div>
<p>其中一个定义面积的方法是利用<a href="/wiki/%E5%85%AC%E7%90%86" title="公理">公理</a>定义。<b>面积</b>可以定义为一个由所有（<a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/%E5%8F%AF%E6%B5%8B%E9%9B%86" title="可测集">可测</a>）平面图形组成的<a href="/wiki/%E9%9B%86%E5%90%88_(%E6%95%B0%E5%AD%A6)" title="集合 (数学)">集合</a><i>M</i>映射至实数的函数<i>a</i>，并满足以下条件：
</p>
<ul><li>对于所有<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle S\in M}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>S</mi>
<mo>∈<!-- ∈ --></mo>
<mi>M</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle S\in M}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="S \in M" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c1128ba57c85e53ae5c172bce085e03686cf0555" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.782ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，有<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a(S)\geq 0}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>S</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mo>≥<!-- ≥ --></mo>
<mn>0</mn>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a(S)\geq 0}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a(S) \ge 0" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/acdc00f97dd6e98df722f8f6c1ebf550b3b323ab" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:8.799ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>。</li>
<li>若<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle S,T\in M}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>S</mi>
<mo>,</mo>
<mi>T</mi>
<mo>∈<!-- ∈ --></mo>
<mi>M</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle S,T\in M}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="S, T \in M" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/6265d6849f07049a4317a67b9796df1dbff4553f" style="vertical-align: -0.671ex; width:9.452ex; height:2.509ex;"/></span>，则<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle S\cup T\in M}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>S</mi>
<mo>∪<!-- ∪ --></mo>
<mi>T</mi>
<mo>∈<!-- ∈ --></mo>
<mi>M</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle S\cup T\in M}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="S \cup T \in M" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/e86727efc7fdb188953c5af1cfdffe8b0f026411" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:11.001ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>及<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle S\cap T\in M}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>S</mi>
<mo>∩<!-- ∩ --></mo>
<mi>T</mi>
<mo>∈<!-- ∈ --></mo>
<mi>M</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle S\cap T\in M}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="S \cap T \in M" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/cbba98ead1150c3852dc8a769a3b227e648a3082" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:11.001ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，且<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a(S\cup T)=a(S)+a(T)-a(S\cap T)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>S</mi>
<mo>∪<!-- ∪ --></mo>
<mi>T</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>a</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>S</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mo>+</mo>
<mi>a</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>T</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mi>a</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>S</mi>
<mo>∩<!-- ∩ --></mo>
<mi>T</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a(S\cup T)=a(S)+a(T)-a(S\cap T)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="a(S \cup T) = a(S) + a(T) - a(S \cap T)" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/5682219ab0493fd07b52ceae5e3325bdbb710172" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:35.507ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>。</li>
<li>若<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle S,T\in M}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</mrow>

</semantics>

</semantics>

<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

<mo>−<!-- − --></mo>
<mi>S</mi>
<mo>∈<!-- ∈ --></mo>
<mi>M</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle T-S\in M}</annotation>
</semantics>

<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>T</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>

<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>S</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a(T-S)=a(T)-a(S)}</annotation>
</semantics>

<li>若<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle S\in M}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="S \in M" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/c1128ba57c85e53ae5c172bce085e03686cf0555" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.782ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>且<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle S}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>S</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle S}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="S" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4611d85173cd3b508e67077d4a1252c9c05abca2" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.499ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>全等于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle T}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>T</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle T}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="T" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ec7200acd984a1d3a3d7dc455e262fbe54f7f6e0" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.636ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，则<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle T\in M}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>T</mi>
<mo>∈<!-- ∈ --></mo>
<mi>M</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle T\in M}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="T \in M" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/026fcb8fb2cb7bdacab3d954f63ae188ae712e2f" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:6.919ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>，且<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a(S)=a(I)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>a</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>S</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
<mo>=</mo>
<mi>a</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>
<mi>I</mi>
<mo stretchy="false">)</mo>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle a(S)=a(I)}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="{\displaystyle a(S)=a(I)}" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4a81d3ecebe63d011f05e0dbba72afb5f2131904" style="vertical-align: -0.838ex; width:11.848ex; height:2.843ex;"/></span>。</li>
<li>任一矩形<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle R}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>R</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle R}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="R" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4b0bfb3769bf24d80e15374dc37b0441e2616e33" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.764ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>均属于<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle M}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>M</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle M}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="M" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f82cade9898ced02fdd08712e5f0c0151758a0dd" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:2.442ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>。若矩形的长为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle \ell }" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>ℓ<!-- ℓ --></mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle \ell }</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="\ell " aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/f066e981e530bacc07efc6a10fa82deee985929e" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:0.97ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>而宽为<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle w}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>w</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="w" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/88b1e0c8e1be5ebe69d18a8010676fa42d7961e6" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.664ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>，则<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a(R)=\ell w}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>

<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>

<mi>w</mi>

<li>设<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle Q}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

</semantics>

</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="c" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/86a67b81c2de995bd608d5b2df50cd8cd7d92455" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.007ex; height:1.676ex;"/></span>，使得所有满足<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle S\subseteq Q\subseteq T}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">

<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">

</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle S}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="S" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/4611d85173cd3b508e67077d4a1252c9c05abca2" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.499ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>及<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle T}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">
<mstyle displaystyle="true" scriptlevel="0">
<mi>T</mi>
</mstyle>
</mrow>
<annotation encoding="application/x-tex">{\displaystyle T}</annotation>
</semantics>
</math></span><img alt="T" aria-hidden="true" class="mwe-math-fallback-image-inline" src="https://wikimedia.org/api/rest_v1/media/math/render/svg/ec7200acd984a1d3a3d7dc455e262fbe54f7f6e0" style="vertical-align: -0.338ex; width:1.636ex; height:2.176ex;"/></span>均有<span class="mwe-math-element"><span class="mwe-math-mathml-inline mwe-math-mathml-a11y" style="display: none;"><math alttext="{\displaystyle a(S)\leq c\leq a(T)}" xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML">
<semantics>
<mrow class="MJX-TeXAtom-ORD">

<mo stretchy="false">(</mo>

</semantics>

<p>可以证明，满足上述条件的函数存在。

<h2><span id=".E5.A4.96.E9.83.A8.E9.80.A3.E7.B5.90"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="外部连结">外部连结</span><span class="mw-editsection"><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">[</span><a href="/w/index.php?title=%E9%9D%A2%E7%A7%AF&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="编辑章节：外部连结">编辑</a><span class="mw-editsection-bracket">]</span></span></h2>
